Additional other non interest expense - Investment Research - $4,732  4.c. During Q3 2022, Glenmede adopted a change in accounting principle to recognize all actuarial gains and losses arising from the periodic remeasurement of its defined benefit pension and postretirement plans immediately; this is commonly referred to as mark-to-market accounting. This change resulted in a cumulative effect adjustment that decreased beginning equity on 1/1/22 by $2.7 million, comprised of $11.4 million decrease in retained earnings, offset by increase in AOCI of $8.6 million.
